Deprecation warning

Use `animate.enter` or `animate.leave` instead. Intent to remove in v23

[API](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#api)

------------------------------------------------------

    function trigger(  name: string,  definitions: AnimationMetadata[],): AnimationTriggerMetadata;

[Usage Notes](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#usage-notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

Define an animation trigger in the `animations` section of `@Component` metadata. In the template, reference the trigger by name and bind it to a trigger expression that evaluates to a defined animation state, using the following format:

`[@triggerName]="expression"`

Animation trigger bindings convert all values to strings, and then match the previous and current values against any linked transitions. Booleans can be specified as `1` or `true` and `0` or `false`.

### [Usage Example](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#usage-example)

The following example creates an animation trigger reference based on the provided name value. The provided animation value is expected to be an array consisting of state and transition declarations.

    @Component({  selector: "my-component",  templateUrl: "my-component-tpl.html",  animations: [    trigger("myAnimationTrigger", [      state(...),      state(...),      transition(...),      transition(...)    ])  ]})class MyComponent {  myStatusExp = "something";}

The template associated with this component makes use of the defined trigger by binding to an element within its template code.

    <!-- somewhere inside of my-component-tpl.html --><div [@myAnimationTrigger]="myStatusExp">...</div>

### [Using an inline function](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#using-an-inline-function)

The `transition` animation method also supports reading an inline function which can decide if its associated animation should be run.

    // this method is run each time the `myAnimationTrigger` trigger value changes.function myInlineMatcherFn(fromState: string, toState: string, element: any, params: {[key:string]: any}): boolean {  // notice that `element` and `params` are also available here  return toState == 'yes-please-animate';}@Component({  selector: 'my-component',  templateUrl: 'my-component-tpl.html',  animations: [    trigger('myAnimationTrigger', [      transition(myInlineMatcherFn, [        // the animation sequence code      ]),    ])  ]})class MyComponent {  myStatusExp = "yes-please-animate";}

### [Disabling Animations](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#disabling-animations)

When true, the special animation control binding `@.disabled` binding prevents all animations from rendering. Place the `@.disabled` binding on an element to disable animations on the element itself, as well as any inner animation triggers within the element.

The following example shows how to use this feature:

    @Component({  selector: 'my-component',  template: `    <div [@.disabled]="isDisabled">      <div [@childAnimation]="exp"></div>    </div>  `,  animations: [    trigger("childAnimation", [      // ...    ])  ]})class MyComponent {  isDisabled = true;  exp = '...';}

When `@.disabled` is true, it prevents the `@childAnimation` trigger from animating, along with any inner animations.

### [Disable animations application-wide](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#disable-animations-application-wide)

When an area of the template is set to have animations disabled, **all** inner components have their animations disabled as well. This means that you can disable all animations for an app by placing a host binding set on `@.disabled` on the topmost Angular component.

    import {Component, HostBinding} from '@angular/core';@Component({  selector: 'app-component',  templateUrl: 'app.component.html',})class AppComponent {  @HostBinding('@.disabled')  public animationsDisabled = true;}

### [Overriding disablement of inner animations](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#overriding-disablement-of-inner-animations)

Despite inner animations being disabled, a parent animation can [`query()`](https://angular.dev/api/animations/query)
 for inner elements located in disabled areas of the template and still animate them if needed. This is also the case for when a sub animation is queried by a parent and then later animated using [`animateChild()`](https://angular.dev/api/animations/animateChild)
.

### [Detecting when an animation is disabled](https://angular.dev/api/animations/trigger#detecting-when-an-animation-is-disabled)

If a region of the DOM (or the entire application) has its animations disabled, the animation trigger callbacks still fire, but for zero seconds. When the callback fires, it provides an instance of an [`AnimationEvent`](https://angular.dev/api/animations/AnimationEvent)
. If animations are disabled, the `.disabled` flag on the event is true.

Jump to details

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult#api)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    ``type [LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]> = {  [I in keyof T]: T[I] extends new (...args: any[]) => infer C // Map `ComponentHarnessConstructor<C>` to `C`.    ? C    : // Map `HarnessPredicate<C>` to `C`.      T[I] extends {harnessType: new (...args: any[]) => infer C}      ? C      : // Map `string` to `TestElement`.        T[I] extends string        ? [TestElement](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement)        : // Map everything else to `never` (should not happen due to the type constraint on `T`).          never;}[number]``
    
    

[Description](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The result type obtained when searching using a particular list of queries. This type depends on the particular items being queried.

*   If one of the queries is for a `ComponentHarnessConstructor<C1>`, it means that the result might be a harness of type `C1`
*   If one of the queries is for a `HarnessPredicate<C2>`, it means that the result might be a harness of type `C2`
*   If one of the queries is for a `string`, it means that the result might be a [`TestElement`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement)
    .

Since we don't know for sure which query will match, the result type if the union of the types for all possible results.

[Usage Notes](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult#usage-notes)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Example](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult#example)

The type:

    LocatorFnResult<[  ComponentHarnessConstructor<MyHarness>,  HarnessPredicate<MyOtherHarness>,  string]>

is equivalent to:

    MyHarness | MyOtherHarness | TestElement

Jump to details

---

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader#api)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    `interface [HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)  {  getChildLoader(selector: string): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >;  getAllChildLoaders(selector: string): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) []>;  getHarness<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<T>;  getHarnessOrNull<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<T | null>;  getHarnessAtIndex<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>, index: number): Promise<T>;  getAllHarnesses<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<T[]>;  countHarnesses<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<number>;  hasHarness<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<boolean>;}`
    
    

Searches for an element with the given selector under the current instances's root element, and returns a [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 rooted at the matching element. If multiple elements match the selector, the first is used. If no elements match, an error is thrown.

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element of the new [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

Searches for all elements with the given selector under the current instances's root element, and returns an array of [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
s, one for each matching element, rooted at that element.

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element of the new [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) []>`

Searches for an instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
's root element, and returns a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for that instance. If multiple matching components are found, a harness for the first one is returned. If no matching component is found, an error is thrown.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<T>`

Searches for an instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
's root element, and returns a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for that instance. If multiple matching components are found, a harness for the first one is returned. If no matching component is found, null is returned.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<T | null>`

Searches for an instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
's root element, and returns a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for the instance on the page at the given index. If no matching component exists at that index, an error is thrown.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@paramindex`number`

The zero-indexed offset of the matching component instance to return

@returns`Promise<T>`

Searches for all instances of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
's root element, and returns a list [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for each instance.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<T[]>`

Searches for all instances of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
's root element, and returns the total count of all matching components.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<number>`

Searches for an instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
's root element, and returns a boolean indicating if any were found.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<boolean>`

Jump to details

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness#api)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    `abstract class [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)  {  constructor(locatorFactory: [LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) ): [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) ;  host(): Promise<[TestElement](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement) >;  protected documentRootLocatorFactory(): [LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) ;  protected locatorFor<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>>;  protected locatorForOptional<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T> | null>;  protected locatorForAll<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>[]>;  protected forceStabilize(): Promise<void>;  protected waitForTasksOutsideAngular(): Promise<void>;}`
    
    

@paramlocatorFactory`[LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) `

@returns`[ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) `

Gets a `Promise` for the [`TestElement`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement)
 representing the host element of the component.

@returns`Promise<[TestElement](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement) >`

Gets a [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)
 for the document root element. This factory can be used to create locators for elements that a component creates outside of its own root element. (e.g. by appending to document.body).

@returns`[LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) `

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the host element of this [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await ch.locatorFor(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await ch.locatorFor('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await ch.locatorFor('span')()            // Throws because the `Promise` rejects

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the host element of this [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await ch.locatorForOptional(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await ch.locatorForOptional('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await ch.locatorForOptional('span')()            // Gets `null`

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T> | null>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instances or elements under the host element of this [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'` and `IdIsD1Harness.hostSelector` is `'#d1'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    // Gets [DivHarness for #d1, TestElement for #d1, DivHarness for #d2, TestElement for #d2]await ch.locatorForAll(DivHarness, 'div')()// Gets [TestElement for #d1, TestElement for #d2]await ch.locatorForAll('div', '#d1')()// Gets [DivHarness for #d1, IdIsD1Harness for #d1, DivHarness for #d2]await ch.locatorForAll(DivHarness, IdIsD1Harness)()// Gets []await ch.locatorForAll('span')()

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>[]>`

Flushes change detection and async tasks in the Angular zone. In most cases it should not be necessary to call this manually. However, there may be some edge cases where it is needed to fully flush animation events.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Waits for all scheduled or running async tasks to complete. This allows harness authors to wait for async tasks outside of the Angular zone.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Jump to details

---

    *   [DragDropModule](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragDropModule)
        
    *   [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef)
        
    *   [DragRefConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig)
        
    *   [DragStartDelay](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragStartDelay)
        
    *   [DropListOrientation](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DropListOrientation)
        
    *   [DropListRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DropListRef)
        
    *   [moveItemInArray](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/moveItemInArray)
        
    *   [Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point)

    *   [transferArrayItem](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/transferArrayItem)
        

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragMove#api)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    `interface [CdkDragMove](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragMove) <T = any> {  source: [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <T>;  pointerPosition: { x: number; y: number; };  event: MouseEvent | TouchEvent;  distance: { x: number; y: number; };  delta: { x: 0 | 1 | -1; y: 0 | 1 | -1; };}`
    
    

Item that is being dragged.

Position of the user's pointer on the page.

Native event that is causing the dragging.

Distance in pixels that the user has dragged since the drag sequence started.

Indicates the direction in which the user is dragging the element along each axis. `1` means that the position is increasing (e.g. the user is moving to the right or downwards), whereas `-1` means that it's decreasing (they're moving to the left or upwards). `0` means that the position hasn't changed.

Jump to details

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragDrop#api)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    `interface [CdkDragDrop](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragDrop) <T, O = T, I = any> {  previousIndex: number;  currentIndex: number;  item: [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <I>;  container: [CdkDropList](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList) <T>;  previousContainer: [CdkDropList](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList) <O>;  isPointerOverContainer: boolean;  distance: { x: number; y: number; };  dropPoint: { x: number; y: number; };  event: MouseEvent | TouchEvent;}`
    
    

Index of the item when it was picked up.

Current index of the item.

Item that is being dropped.

Container in which the item was dropped.

Container from which the item was picked up. Can be the same as the `container`.

Whether the user's pointer was over the container when the item was dropped.

Distance in pixels that the user has dragged since the drag sequence started.

Position where the pointer was when the item was dropped

Native event that caused the drop event.

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate#api)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    `class [HarnessPredicate](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate) <T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) > {  constructor(harnessType: [ComponentHarnessConstructor](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarnessConstructor) <T>, options: [BaseHarnessFilters](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/BaseHarnessFilters) ): [HarnessPredicate](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate) <T>;  override harnessType: [ComponentHarnessConstructor](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarnessConstructor) <T>;  add(description: string, predicate: [AsyncPredicate](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/AsyncPredicate) <T>): this;  addOption<O>(name: string, option: O | undefined, predicate: [AsyncOptionPredicate](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/AsyncOptionPredicate) <T, O>): this;  filter(harnesses: T[]): Promise<T[]>;  evaluate(harness: T): Promise<boolean>;  getDescription(): string;  getSelector(): string;  static stringMatches(value: string | Promise<string | null> | null, pattern: string | RegExp | null): Promise<boolean>;}`
    
    

@paramharnessType`[ComponentHarnessConstructor](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarnessConstructor) <T>`

@paramoptions`[BaseHarnessFilters](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/BaseHarnessFilters) `

@returns`[HarnessPredicate](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate) <T>`

Adds a predicate function to be run against candidate harnesses.

@paramdescription`string`

A description of this predicate that may be used in error messages.

@parampredicate`[AsyncPredicate](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/AsyncPredicate) <T>`

An async predicate function.

@returns`this`

Adds a predicate function that depends on an option value to be run against candidate harnesses. If the option value is undefined, the predicate will be ignored.

@paramname`string`

The name of the option (may be used in error messages).

@paramoption`O | undefined`

The option value.

@parampredicate`[AsyncOptionPredicate](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/AsyncOptionPredicate) <T, O>`

The predicate function to run if the option value is not undefined.

@returns`this`

Filters a list of harnesses on this predicate.

@paramharnesses`T[]`

The list of harnesses to filter.

@returns`Promise<T[]>`

Evaluates whether the given harness satisfies this predicate.

@paramharness`T`

The harness to check

@returns`Promise<boolean>`

Gets a description of this predicate for use in error messages.

@returns`string`

Gets the selector used to find candidate elements.

@returns`string`

Checks if the specified nullable string value matches the given pattern.

@paramvalue`string | Promise<string | null> | null`

The nullable string value to check, or a Promise resolving to the nullable string value.

@parampattern`string | RegExp | null`

The pattern the value is expected to match. If `pattern` is a string, `value` is expected to match exactly. If `pattern` is a regex, a partial match is allowed. If `pattern` is `null`, the value is expected to be `null`.

@returns`Promise<boolean>`

Deprecation warning

Use the [`createDragRef`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/createDragRef)
 or [`createDropListRef`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/createDropListRef)
 function for better tree shaking. Will be removed in v23.

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragDrop#api)

----------------------------------------------------------

    `class [DragDrop](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragDrop)  {  createDrag<T = any>(element: any, config?: [DragRefConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig)  | undefined): [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <T>;  createDropList<T = any>(element: any): [DropListRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DropListRef) <T>;}`
    
    

Turns an element into a draggable item.

@deprecated

Use the [`createDragRef`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/createDragRef)
 function that provides better tree shaking.

@paramelement`any`

Element to which to attach the dragging functionality.

@paramconfig`[DragRefConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig)  | undefined`

Object used to configure the dragging behavior.

@returns`[DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <T>`

Turns an element into a drop list.

@deprecated

Use the [`createDropListRef`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/createDropListRef)
 function that provides better tree shaking.

@paramelement`any`

Element to which to attach the drop list functionality.

@returns`[DropListRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DropListRef) <T>`

Jump to details

---

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ContentContainerComponentHarness#api)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    `abstract class [ContentContainerComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ContentContainerComponentHarness) <S extends string = string> extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)  implements [HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)  {  getChildLoader(selector: S): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >;  getAllChildLoaders(selector: S): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) []>;  getHarness<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<T>;  getHarnessOrNull<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<T | null>;  getHarnessAtIndex<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>, index: number): Promise<T>;  getAllHarnesses<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<T[]>;  countHarnesses<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<number>;  hasHarness<T extends [ComponentHarness](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness) >(query: [HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>): Promise<boolean>;  protected getRootHarnessLoader(): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >;  override host(): Promise<[TestElement](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement) >;  protected override documentRootLocatorFactory(): [LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) ;  protected override locatorFor<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>>;  protected override locatorForOptional<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T> | null>;  protected override forceStabilize(): Promise<void>;  protected override waitForTasksOutsideAngular(): Promise<void>;}`
    
    

Gets a [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 that searches for harnesses under the first element matching the given selector within the current harness's content.

@paramselector`S`

The selector for an element in the component's content.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

Gets a list of [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 for each element matching the given selector under the current harness's cotnent that searches for harnesses under that element.

@paramselector`S`

The selector for elements in the component's content.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) []>`

Gets the first matching harness for the given query within the current harness's content.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

The harness query to search for.

@returns`Promise<T>`

Gets the first matching harness for the given query within the current harness's content.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

The harness query to search for.

@returns`Promise<T | null>`

Gets a matching harness for the given query and index within the current harness's content.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

The harness query to search for.

@paramindex`number`

The zero-indexed offset of the component to find.

@returns`Promise<T>`

Gets all matching harnesses for the given query within the current harness's content.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

The harness query to search for.

@returns`Promise<T[]>`

Returns the number of matching harnesses for the given query within the current harness's content.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

The harness query to search for.

@returns`Promise<number>`

Checks whether there is a matching harnesses for the given query within the current harness's content.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

The harness query to search for.

@returns`Promise<boolean>`

Gets the root harness loader from which to start searching for content contained by this harness.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

Gets a `Promise` for the [`TestElement`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement)
 representing the host element of the component.

@returns`Promise<[TestElement](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement) >`

Gets a [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)
 for the document root element. This factory can be used to create locators for elements that a component creates outside of its own root element. (e.g. by appending to document.body).

@returns`[LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) `

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the host element of this [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await ch.locatorFor(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await ch.locatorFor('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await ch.locatorFor('span')()            // Throws because the `Promise` rejects

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the host element of this [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await ch.locatorForOptional(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await ch.locatorForOptional('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await ch.locatorForOptional('span')()            // Gets `null`

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T> | null>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instances or elements under the host element of this [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'` and `IdIsD1Harness.hostSelector` is `'#d1'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    // Gets [DivHarness for #d1, TestElement for #d1, DivHarness for #d2, TestElement for #d2]await ch.locatorForAll(DivHarness, 'div')()// Gets [TestElement for #d1, TestElement for #d2]await ch.locatorForAll('div', '#d1')()// Gets [DivHarness for #d1, IdIsD1Harness for #d1, DivHarness for #d2]await ch.locatorForAll(DivHarness, IdIsD1Harness)()// Gets []await ch.locatorForAll('span')()

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>[]>`

Flushes change detection and async tasks in the Angular zone. In most cases it should not be necessary to call this manually. However, there may be some edge cases where it is needed to fully flush animation events.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Waits for all scheduled or running async tasks to complete. This allows harness authors to wait for async tasks outside of the Angular zone.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Jump to details

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragDropConfig#api)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    `interface [DragDropConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragDropConfig)  extends Partial<[DragRefConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig) > {  lockAxis?: [DragAxis](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragAxis)  | null | undefined;  dragStartDelay?: [DragStartDelay](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragStartDelay)  | undefined;  constrainPosition?: [DragConstrainPosition](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragConstrainPosition)  | undefined;  previewClass?: string | string[] | undefined;  boundaryElement?: string | undefined;  rootElementSelector?: string | undefined;  draggingDisabled?: boolean | undefined;  sortingDisabled?: boolean | undefined;  listAutoScrollDisabled?: boolean | undefined;  listOrientation?: [DropListOrientation](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DropListOrientation)  | undefined;  zIndex?: number | undefined;  previewContainer?: "global" | "parent" | undefined;  override dragStartThreshold: number;  override pointerDirectionChangeThreshold: number;  override parentDragRef?: [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <any> | undefined;}`
    
    

Minimum amount of pixels that the user should drag, before the CDK initiates a drag sequence.

Amount the pixels the user should drag before the CDK considers them to have changed the drag direction.

Ref that the current drag item is nested in.

Jump to details

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig#api)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    `interface [DragRefConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig)  {  dragStartThreshold: number;  pointerDirectionChangeThreshold: number;  zIndex?: number | undefined;  parentDragRef?: [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <any> | undefined;}`
    
    

Minimum amount of pixels that the user should drag, before the CDK initiates a drag sequence.

Amount the pixels the user should drag before the CDK considers them to have changed the drag direction.

`z-index` for the absolutely-positioned elements that are created by the drag item.

Ref that the current drag item is nested in.

Jump to details

---

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragEnd#api)

------------------------------------------------------------

    `interface [CdkDragEnd](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragEnd) <T = any> {  source: [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <T>;  distance: { x: number; y: number; };  dropPoint: { x: number; y: number; };  event: MouseEvent | TouchEvent;}`
    
    

Draggable that emitted the event.

Distance in pixels that the user has dragged since the drag sequence started.

Position where the pointer was when the item was dropped

Native event that caused the dragging to stop.

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/parallel#api)

--------------------------------------------------------

    function parallel<T1, T2, T3, T4, T5>(  values: () => [    T1 | PromiseLike<T1>,    T2 | PromiseLike<T2>,    T3 | PromiseLike<T3>,    T4 | PromiseLike<T4>,    T5 | PromiseLike<T5>,  ],): Promise<[T1, T2, T3, T4, T5]>;function parallel<T1, T2, T3, T4>(  values: () => [    T1 | PromiseLike<T1>,    T2 | PromiseLike<T2>,    T3 | PromiseLike<T3>,    T4 | PromiseLike<T4>,  ],): Promise<[T1, T2, T3, T4]>;function parallel<T1, T2, T3>(  values: () => [    T1 | PromiseLike<T1>,    T2 | PromiseLike<T2>,    T3 | PromiseLike<T3>,  ],): Promise<[T1, T2, T3]>;function parallel<T1, T2>(  values: () => [T1 | PromiseLike<T1>, T2 | PromiseLike<T2>],): Promise<[T1, T2]>;function parallel<T>(values: () => (T | PromiseLike<T>)[]): Promise<T[]>;

Resolves the given list of async values in parallel (i.e. via Promise.all) while batching change detection over the entire operation such that change detection occurs exactly once before resolving the values and once after.

@paramvalues`() => [T1 | PromiseLike<T1>, T2 | PromiseLike<T2>, T3 | PromiseLike<T3>, T4 | PromiseLike<T4>, T5 | PromiseLike<T5>]`

A getter for the async values to resolve in parallel with batched change detection.

@returns`Promise<[T1, T2, T3, T4, T5]>`

Resolves the given list of async values in parallel (i.e. via Promise.all) while batching change detection over the entire operation such that change detection occurs exactly once before resolving the values and once after.

@paramvalues`() => [T1 | PromiseLike<T1>, T2 | PromiseLike<T2>, T3 | PromiseLike<T3>, T4 | PromiseLike<T4>]`

A getter for the async values to resolve in parallel with batched change detection.

@returns`Promise<[T1, T2, T3, T4]>`

Resolves the given list of async values in parallel (i.e. via Promise.all) while batching change detection over the entire operation such that change detection occurs exactly once before resolving the values and once after.

@paramvalues`() => [T1 | PromiseLike<T1>, T2 | PromiseLike<T2>, T3 | PromiseLike<T3>]`

A getter for the async values to resolve in parallel with batched change detection.

@returns`Promise<[T1, T2, T3]>`

Resolves the given list of async values in parallel (i.e. via Promise.all) while batching change detection over the entire operation such that change detection occurs exactly once before resolving the values and once after.

@paramvalues`() => [T1 | PromiseLike<T1>, T2 | PromiseLike<T2>]`

A getter for the async values to resolve in parallel with batched change detection.

@returns`Promise<[T1, T2]>`

Resolves the given list of async values in parallel (i.e. via Promise.all) while batching change detection over the entire operation such that change detection occurs exactly once before resolving the values and once after.

@paramvalues`() => (T | PromiseLike<T>)[]`

A getter for the async values to resolve in parallel with batched change detection.

@returns`Promise<T[]>`

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory#api)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    `interface [LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)  {  documentRootLocatorFactory(): [LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) ;  rootElement: [TestElement](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement) ;  locatorFor<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>>;  locatorForOptional<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T> | null>;  locatorForAll<T extends ([HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <any> | string)[]>(...queries: T): () => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>[]>;  rootHarnessLoader(): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >;  harnessLoaderFor(selector: string): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >;  harnessLoaderForOptional(selector: string): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)  | null>;  harnessLoaderForAll(selector: string): Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) []>;  forceStabilize(): Promise<void>;  waitForTasksOutsideAngular(): Promise<void>;}`
    
    

Gets a locator factory rooted at the document root.

@returns`[LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) `

The root element of this [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)
 as a [`TestElement`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement)
.

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the root element of this [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await lf.locatorFor(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await lf.locatorFor('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await lf.locatorFor('span')()            // Throws because the `Promise` rejects

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the root element of this [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await lf.locatorForOptional(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await lf.locatorForOptional('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await lf.locatorForOptional('span')()            // Gets `null`

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T> | null>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instances or elements under the root element of this [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'` and `IdIsD1Harness.hostSelector` is `'#d1'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    // Gets [DivHarness for #d1, TestElement for #d1, DivHarness for #d2, TestElement for #d2]await lf.locatorForAll(DivHarness, 'div')()// Gets [TestElement for #d1, TestElement for #d2]await lf.locatorForAll('div', '#d1')()// Gets [DivHarness for #d1, IdIsD1Harness for #d1, DivHarness for #d2]await lf.locatorForAll(DivHarness, IdIsD1Harness)()// Gets []await lf.locatorForAll('span')()

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>[]>`

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

Gets a [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 instance for an element under the root of this [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)
.

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

Gets a [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 instance for an element under the root of this [`LocatorFactory`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)  | null>`

Gets a list of [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 instances, one for each matching element.

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) []>`

Flushes change detection and async tasks captured in the Angular zone. In most cases it should not be necessary to call this manually. However, there may be some edge cases where it is needed to fully flush animation events.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Waits for all scheduled or running async tasks to complete. This allows harness authors to wait for async tasks outside of the Angular zone.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Jump to details

---

    `abstract class [HarnessEnvironment](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment) <E> implements [HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)  ,[LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory)  {  protected constructor(rawRootElement: E): [HarnessEnvironment](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment) <E>; @paramrawRootElement`E`

The native root element of this [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
.

@returns`[HarnessEnvironment](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment) <E>`

The root element of this [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
 as a [`TestElement`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/TestElement)
.

Gets a locator factory rooted at the document root.

@returns`[LocatorFactory](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFactory) `

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the root element of this [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await lf.locatorFor(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await lf.locatorFor('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await lf.locatorFor('span')()            // Throws because the `Promise` rejects

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instance or element under the root element of this `HarnessEnvironmnet`.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    await lf.locatorForOptional(DivHarness, 'div')() // Gets a `DivHarness` instance for #d1await lf.locatorForOptional('div', DivHarness)() // Gets a `TestElement` instance for #d1await lf.locatorForOptional('span')()            // Gets `null`

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T> | null>`

Creates an asynchronous locator function that can be used to find [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 instances or elements under the root element of this [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
.

For example, given the following DOM and assuming `DivHarness.hostSelector` is `'div'` and `IdIsD1Harness.hostSelector` is `'#d1'`

    <div id="d1"></div><div id="d2"></div>

then we expect:

    // Gets [DivHarness for #d1, TestElement for #d1, DivHarness for #d2, TestElement for #d2]await lf.locatorForAll(DivHarness, 'div')()// Gets [TestElement for #d1, TestElement for #d2]await lf.locatorForAll('div', '#d1')()// Gets [DivHarness for #d1, IdIsD1Harness for #d1, DivHarness for #d2]await lf.locatorForAll(DivHarness, IdIsD1Harness)()// Gets []await lf.locatorForAll('span')()

@paramqueries`T`

A list of queries specifying which harnesses and elements to search for:

*   A `string` searches for elements matching the CSS selector specified by the string.
*   A [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     constructor searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given class.
*   A [`HarnessPredicate`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessPredicate)
     searches for [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
     instances matching the given predicate.

@returns`() => Promise<[LocatorFnResult](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/LocatorFnResult) <T>[]>`

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

Gets a [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 instance for an element under the root of this [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
.

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

Gets a [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 instance for an element under the root of this [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
.

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)  | null>`

Gets a list of [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 instances, one for each matching element.

@paramselector`string`

The selector for the root element.

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) []>`

Searches for an instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
's root element, and returns a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for that instance. If multiple matching components are found, a harness for the first one is returned. If no matching component is found, an error is thrown.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<T>`

Searches for an instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
's root element, and returns a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for that instance. If multiple matching components are found, a harness for the first one is returned. If no matching component is found, null is returned.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<T | null>`

Searches for an instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type and index under the [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
's root element, and returns a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for that instance. The index specifies the offset of the component to find. If no matching component is found at that index, an error is thrown.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@paramoffset`number`

@returns`Promise<T>`

Searches for all instances of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
's root element, and returns a list [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for each instance.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

A query for a harness to create

@returns`Promise<T[]>`

Searches for all instance of the component corresponding to the given harness type under the [`HarnessEnvironment`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessEnvironment)
's root element, and returns the number that were found.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

@returns`Promise<number>`

's root element, and returns a boolean indicating if any were found.

@paramquery`[HarnessQuery](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessQuery) <T>`

@returns`Promise<boolean>`

Searches for an element with the given selector under the evironment's root element, and returns a [`HarnessLoader`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader)
 rooted at the matching element. If multiple elements match the selector, the first is used. If no elements match, an error is thrown.

@paramselector`string`

@returns`Promise<[HarnessLoader](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/HarnessLoader) >`

@paramselector`string`

Creates a [`ComponentHarness`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarness)
 for the given harness type with the given raw host element.

@paramharnessType`[ComponentHarnessConstructor](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/testing/ComponentHarnessConstructor) <T>`

@paramelement`E`

@returns`T`

Flushes change detection and async tasks captured in the Angular zone. In most cases it should not be necessary to call this manually. However, there may be some edge cases where it is needed to fully flush animation events. This is an abstrct method that must be implemented by subclasses.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Waits for all scheduled or running async tasks to complete. This allows harness authors to wait for async tasks outside of the Angular zone. This is an abstrct method that must be implemented by subclasses.

@returns`Promise<void>`

Gets the root element for the document.

 from a raw element.

 rooted at the given raw element.

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList#api)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    `class [CdkDropList](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList) <T = any> implements [OnDestroy](https://angular.dev/api/core/OnDestroy)  {  element: any;  connectedTo: string | [CdkDropList](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList) <any> | (string | [CdkDropList](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList) <any>)[];  data: T;  orientation: [DropListOrientation](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DropListOrientation) ;  id: string;  lockAxis: [DragAxis](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragAxis)  | null;   get disabled(): boolean;  sortingDisabled: boolean;  enterPredicate: (drag: [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>, drop: [CdkDropList](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList) <any>) => boolean;  sortPredicate: (index: number, drag: [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>, drop: [CdkDropList](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList) <any>) => boolean;  autoScrollDisabled: boolean;  autoScrollStep: NumberInput;  elementContainerSelector: string | null;  hasAnchor: boolean;  readonly dropped: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragDrop](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragDrop) <T, any, any>>;  readonly entered: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragEnter](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragEnter) <T, T>>;  readonly exited: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragExit](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragExit) <T, T>>;  readonly sorted: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragSortEvent](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragSortEvent) <T, T>>;  addItem(item: [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>): void;  removeItem(item: [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>): void;  getSortedItems(): [CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>[];}`
    
    

Other draggable containers that this container is connected to and into which the container's items can be transferred. Can either be references to other drop containers, or their unique IDs.

Arbitrary data to attach to this container.

Direction in which the list is oriented.

Unique ID for the drop zone. Can be used as a reference in the `connectedTo` of another [`CdkDropList`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDropList)
.

Locks the position of the draggable elements inside the container along the specified axis.

Whether starting a dragging sequence from this container is disabled.

Whether sorting within this drop list is disabled.

Function that is used to determine whether an item is allowed to be moved into a drop container.

Functions that is used to determine whether an item can be sorted into a particular index.

Whether to auto-scroll the view when the user moves their pointer close to the edges.

Number of pixels to scroll for each frame when auto-scrolling an element.

Selector that will be used to resolve an alternate element container for the drop list. Passing an alternate container is useful for the cases where one might not have control over the parent node of the draggable items within the list (e.g. due to content projection). This allows for usages like:

    <div cdkDropList cdkDropListElementContainer=".inner">  <div class="inner">    <div cdkDrag></div>  </div></div>

By default when an item leaves its initial container, its placeholder will be transferred to the new container. If that's not desirable for your use case, you can enable this option which will clone the placeholder and leave it inside the original container. If the item is returned to the initial container, the anchor element will be removed automatically.

The cloned placeholder can be styled by targeting the `cdk-drag-anchor` class.

This option is useful in combination with `cdkDropListSortingDisabled` to implement copying behavior in a drop list.

Emits when the user drops an item inside the container.

Emits when the user has moved a new drag item into this container.

Emits when the user removes an item from the container by dragging it into another container.

Emits as the user is swapping items while actively dragging.

Registers an items with the drop list.

@paramitem`[CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>`

@returns`void`

Removes an item from the drop list.

@paramitem`[CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>`

@returns`void`

Gets the registered items in the list, sorted by their position in the DOM.

@returns`[CdkDrag](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag) <any>[]`

@returns`void`

 readonly released: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragRelease](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragRelease) <any>>;  readonly ended: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragEnd](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragEnd) <any>>;  readonly entered: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragEnter](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragEnter) <any, any>>;  readonly exited: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragExit](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragExit) <any, any>>;  readonly dropped: [EventEmitter](https://angular.dev/api/core/EventEmitter) <[CdkDragDrop](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragDrop) <any, any, any>>;  readonly moved: Observable<[CdkDragMove](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDragMove) <T>>;  getPlaceholderElement(): HTMLElement;  getRootElement(): HTMLElement;  reset(): void;  resetToBoundary(): void;  getFreeDragPosition(): Readonly<[Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point) >;  setFreeDragPosition(value: [Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point) ): void;}`
    
    

Arbitrary data to attach to this drag instance.

Locks the position of the dragged element along the specified axis.

Selector that will be used to determine the root draggable element, starting from the `cdkDrag` element and going up the DOM. Passing an alternate root element is useful when trying to enable dragging on an element that you might not have access to.

Node or selector that will be used to determine the element to which the draggable's position will be constrained. If a string is passed in, it'll be used as a selector that will be matched starting from the element's parent and going up the DOM until a match has been found.

Amount of milliseconds to wait after the user has put their pointer down before starting to drag the element.

Sets the position of a [`CdkDrag`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CdkDrag)
 that is outside of a drop container. Can be used to restore the element's position for a returning user.

Whether starting to drag this element is disabled.

Function that can be used to customize the logic of how the position of the drag item is limited while it's being dragged. Gets called with a point containing the current position of the user's pointer on the page, a reference to the item being dragged and its dimensions. Should return a point describing where the item should be rendered.

Class to be added to the preview element.

Configures the place into which the preview of the item will be inserted. Can be configured globally through [`CDK_DROP_LIST`](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/CDK_DROP_LIST)
. Possible values:

*   `global` - Preview will be inserted at the bottom of the `<body>`. The advantage is that you don't have to worry about `overflow: hidden` or `z-index`, but the item won't retain its inherited styles.
*   `parent` - Preview will be inserted into the parent of the drag item. The advantage is that inherited styles will be preserved, but it may be clipped by `overflow: hidden` or not be visible due to `z-index`. Furthermore, the preview is going to have an effect over selectors like `:nth-child` and some flexbox configurations.
*   `ElementRef<HTMLElement> | HTMLElement` - Preview will be inserted into a specific element. Same advantages and disadvantages as `parent`.

If the parent of the dragged element has a `scale` transform, it can throw off the positioning when the user starts dragging. Use this input to notify the CDK of the scale.

Emits when the user starts dragging the item.

Emits when the user has released a drag item, before any animations have started.

Emits when the user stops dragging an item in the container.

Emits when the user has moved the item into a new container.

Emits when the user removes the item its container by dragging it into another container.

Emits when the user drops the item inside a container.

Emits as the user is dragging the item. Use with caution, because this event will fire for every pixel that the user has dragged.

Returns the element that is being used as a placeholder while the current element is being dragged.

@returns`HTMLElement`

Returns the root draggable element.

@returns`HTMLElement`

Resets a standalone drag item to its initial position.

@returns`void`

Resets drag item to end of boundary element.

@returns`void`

Gets the pixel coordinates of the draggable outside of a drop container.

@returns`Readonly<[Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point) >`

Sets the current position in pixels the draggable outside of a drop container.

@paramvalue`[Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point) `

New position to be set.

@returns`void`

@returns`void`

@paramchanges`[SimpleChanges](https://angular.dev/api/core/SimpleChanges) `

@returns`void`

@returns`void`

Jump to details

Element that the drop list is attached to.

Whether starting a dragging sequence from this container is disabled.

Whether sorting items within the list is disabled.

Locks the position of the draggable elements inside the container along the specified axis.

Whether auto-scrolling the view when the user moves their pointer close to the edges is disabled.

Number of pixels to scroll for each frame when auto-scrolling an element.

Whether the items in the list should leave an anchor node when leaving the initial container.

Function that is used to determine whether an item is allowed to be moved into a drop container.

Function that is used to determine whether an item can be sorted into a particular index.

Emits right before dragging has started.

Emits when the user has moved a new drag item into this container.

Emits when the user removes an item from the container by dragging it into another container.

Emits when the user drops an item inside the container.

Emits as the user is swapping items while actively dragging.

Emits when a dragging sequence is started in a list connected to the current one.

Emits when a dragging sequence is stopped from a list connected to the current one.

Arbitrary data that can be attached to the drop list.

Removes the drop list functionality from the DOM element.

@returns`void`

Whether an item from this list is currently being dragged.

@returns`boolean`

Starts dragging an item.

@returns`void`

Attempts to move an item into the container.

Item that was moved into the container.

Position of the item along the X axis.

@parampointerY`number`

Position of the item along the Y axis.

@paramindex`number | undefined`

Index at which the item entered. If omitted, the container will try to figure it out automatically.

@returns`void`

Removes an item from the container after it was dragged into another container by the user.

@paramitem`[DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <any>`

Item that was dragged out.

@returns`void`

@paramdirection`Direction`

Elements that can be scrolled.

@returns`this`

Configures the drop list so that a different element is used as the container for the dragged items. This is useful for the cases when one might not have control over the full DOM that sets up the dragging. Note that the alternate container needs to be a descendant of the drop list.

@paramcontainer`HTMLElement`

[API](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef#api)

---------------------------------------------------------

    `class [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <T = any> {  constructor(element: any, _config: [DragRefConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig) , _document: Document, _ngZone: [NgZone](https://angular.dev/api/core/NgZone) , _viewportRuler: ViewportRuler, _dragDropRegistry: [DragDropRegistry](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragDropRegistry) , _renderer: [Renderer2](https://angular.dev/api/core/Renderer2) ): [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <T>;  lockAxis: "x" | "y" | null;  dragStartDelay: number | { touch: number; mouse: number; };  previewClass: string | string[] | undefined;  scale: number;   get disabled(): boolean;  readonly beforeStarted: any;  readonly started: any;  readonly released: any;  readonly ended: any;  readonly entered: any;  readonly exited: any;  readonly dropped: any;  readonly moved: Observable<{ source: [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <any>; pointerPosition: { x: number; y: number; }; event: MouseEvent | TouchEvent; distance: [Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point) ; delta: { x: 0 | 1 | -1; y: 0 | 1 | -1; }; }>;  data: T;  constrainPosition?: [DragConstrainPosition](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragConstrainPosition)  | undefined;  getPlaceholderElement(): HTMLElement;  getRootElement(): HTMLElement;  getVisibleElement(): HTMLElement;  withHandles(handles: any[]): this;  withPreviewTemplate(template: DragPreviewTemplate<any> | null): this;  withPlaceholderTemplate(template: DragHelperTemplate<any> | null): this;  withRootElement(rootElement: any): this;  withBoundaryElement(boundaryElement: any): this;  withParent(parent: [DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <unknown> | null): this;  dispose(): void;  isDragging(): boolean;  reset(): void;  resetToBoundary(): void;  disableHandle(handle: HTMLElement): void;  enableHandle(handle: HTMLElement): void;  withDirection(direction: Direction): this;  getFreeDragPosition(): Readonly<[Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point) >;  setFreeDragPosition(value: [Point](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/Point) ): this;  withPreviewContainer(value: any): this;}`
    
    

@paramelement`any`

@param\_config`[DragRefConfig](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRefConfig) `

@param\_document`Document`

@param\_ngZone`[NgZone](https://angular.dev/api/core/NgZone) `

@param\_viewportRuler`ViewportRuler`

@param\_dragDropRegistry`[DragDropRegistry](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragDropRegistry) `

@param\_renderer`[Renderer2](https://angular.dev/api/core/Renderer2) `

@returns`[DragRef](https://angular.dev/api/cdk/drag-drop/DragRef) <T>`

Axis along which dragging is locked.

Amount of milliseconds to wait after the user has put their pointer down before starting to drag the element.

Class to be added to the preview element.

If the parent of the dragged element has a `scale` transform, it can throw off the positioning when the user starts dragging. Use this input to notify the CDK of the scale.

Whether starting to drag this element is disabled.

Emits as the drag sequence is being prepared.

Emits when the user starts dragging the item.

Emits when the user has released a drag item, before any animations have started.

Emits when the user stops dragging an item in the container.

Emits when the user has moved the item into a new container.

Emits when the user removes the item its container by dragging it into another container.

Emits when the user drops the item inside a container.

Emits as the user is dragging the item. Use with caution, because this event will fire for every pixel that the user has dragged.

Arbitrary data that can be attached to the drag item.

Function that can be used to customize the logic of how the position of the drag item is limited while it's being dragged. Gets called with a point containing the current position of the user's pointer on the page, a reference to the item being dragged and its dimensions. Should return a point describing where the item should be rendered.

Returns the element that is being used as a placeholder while the current element is being dragged.

@returns`HTMLElement`

Returns the root draggable element.

@returns`HTMLElement`

Gets the currently-visible element that represents the drag item. While dragging this is the placeholder, otherwise it's the root element.

@returns`HTMLElement`

Registers the handles that can be used to drag the element.

@returns`this`

Sets an alternate drag root element. The root element is the element that will be moved as the user is dragging. Passing an alternate root element is useful when trying to enable dragging on an element that you might not have access to.

@paramrootElement`any`

@returns`this`

@returns`this`

Removes the dragging functionality from the DOM element.

Resets a standalone drag item to its initial position.

@returns`void`

@returns`void`

@returns`void`
